@## / /
rgya gar skad du /
bud+d+ha tsa ri ta ma hA kA bya nA ma /
bod skad du /
sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po /
sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo / /
dpal ldan yon tan tshogs kyis gang / /
bdag nyid chen po sems can gyi / /
don mdzad yang dag sangs rgyas dang / /
chos dang dge 'dun la phyag 'tshal / /
bu ram shing par mthu mnyam bu ram shing ba'i rgyud / /
thub dka' shAkya rnams la spyod pa rnam dag pa / /
'phrog byed zla ba lta bur skye dgu rnams la sdug /
rgyal po zas gtsang zhes bya'i ming can byung bar gyur / /
dbang po dang mtshungs de yi bdag po ldan ma yin / /
nus mthu rjes mtshungs gzi brjid lha mo bde sogs dang / /
pad+mo can 'dra phun sum tshogs pa sa bzhin brtan / /
sgyu ma chen mo zhes bya dpe med sgyu 'dra byung / /
mi skyong rgyal po 'di ni de dang thabs cig tu / /
dga' ba nyer ldan rnam thos sras kyi dpal bzhin rol / /
de nas yang dag ting 'dzin ldan pa'i rig ma bzhin / /
sdig bral ma de mngal ni rnam par gzung bar gyur / /
mngal dang nye bar ldan pa nyid kyi sngon rol du / /
de ni gnyid song glang po'i dbang po dkar po zhig /
rang nyid la ni rab tu zhugs sogs mthong gyur la / /
de yi mtshan ma nyam thag pa nas thob ma yin / /
lha dang rab tu mtshungs pa de yi lha mo de / /
mngal gyis rigs kyi dpal ni rab tu 'dren byed cing / /
sgyu ma ngal ba dang ni mya ngan sgyu med par / /
gtsang la nyon mongs med pa'i dgon par blo gros mdzad / /
de ni lum bi zhes bya'i nags mthar gyur pa'i sa / /
sna tshogs ljon shing sna tshogs shing rta mngon dga' bar / /
bsam gtan la bzod dben pa'i nags kyi mtha' bzhed ma / /
'gro ba'i chad dang gnas phyir mi skyong la zhus so / /
de yi chos dang ldan la 'phags pa'i zhes 'dod dag /
rnam par shes nas ya mtshan dga' ba yis gang ste / /
zhi ba'i grong nas sa yi bdag po gshegs gyur te / /
de yi dga' ba'i rgyu yin rnam par rgyu phyir min / /
dpal dang ldan pa'i nags der rgyal po'i bdag ldan ma / /
rab tu bltam pa'i dus ni yang dag mngon gzigs shing / /
bla re nye bar phul ba'i gzims mal rab thob ste / /
mi mo stong phrag dag gis mngon par dga' bar byed / /
de nas skar ma rgyal rab ldan par gyur pa'i tshe / /
brtul zhugs legs par 'dus byas lha mo de yi ni / /
rtsib logs dag nas 'jig rten phan phyir sras bltams te / /
tshor ba dang ni bral zhing nad dang bral ba nyid / /
ji ltar brla skyes brla nas rgya chen lag pa nas / /
dbang po dang mtshungs nga la nu ni spyi bo nas / /
mtshan ldan nyid kyang lag pa'i cha shas gsang ba nas / /
rnam pa de ltar de yi skye ba byung bar gyur / /
mngal nas mngon par nges par byung ba gzugs mdzes te / /
nam mkha' dag las 'phros 'dra skye gnas las ma skyes / /
bskal ba gcig min rnams su bsgoms pa'i bdag nyid ni / /
gang zhig yang dag rab tu shes na skyes gyur blun po min / /
nyi ma gzhon nu sa lam mngon par babs pa bzhin / /
gsal ba dang ni brtan pas gang zhig mdzes pa ste / /
de ltar shin tu gsal yang nges par rtog pa na / /
ri bong gis mtshan ji ltar mig dag 'phrogs par gyur / /
de ni rang gi lus kyi 'od rab 'bar ba yis / /
sgron ma'i 'od kyang gsal bar byed pa ltar bcom ste / /
rin thang chen po 'dzam bu chu gser mdzes pa'i mdog /
phyogs rnams thams cad rnam par snang zhing gsal bar mdzad / /
'khrugs pa ma yin yon po'i skyon dag rab bsal zhing / /
shin tu brtan pa dang ldan rnam par yangs pa'i 'gros / /
de ltar mi g.yo rab tu brtan pa'i gom pa bdun / /
drang srong skar ma bdun dang rab mnyam gshegs par gyur / /
byang chub phyir dang 'gro la phan pa'i phyir skyes shing / /
'di ni bdag gi srid pa'i skye ba tha ma zhes / /
seng ge'i 'gros 'dra phyogs bzhi dag tu rnam gzigs nas / /
snod ldan rnams kyi don byed dag kyang smras par gyur / /
nam mkha' dag las rab babs zla ba'i 'od zer dkar / /
grang dang dro ba'i chu rgyun rnam pa gnyis kyi shugs / /
lus la yang dag reg pas bde ba bskyed pa'i phyir / /
mdzes shing yid 'ong de yi spyi bor babs par gyur / /
dpal ldan bla re bres par gser gyis 'bar zhing mtshan / /
bai DUR+Ya yi rkang pa'i gzims mal la gzims pa / /
de la gus phyir gser gyi pad+ma'i phyag mnga' ba'i / /
gnod sbyin bdag rnams kun nas yongs su bskor nas gnas / /
mi mngon gyur pa'i lha rnams kyis kyang nam mkha' la / /
gang gi mthu las mgo bo yis ni rab btud cing / /
kun nas gdung ba skyob pa'i gdugs dkar rnams bzung ste / /
byang chub ched du mchog gi bsngags pa dag kyang smras / /
'das pa'i sangs rgyas rnams la lhag par mchod byas pa'i / /
lto 'phye che rnams khyad 'phags chos la sred pa'i phyir / /
gang la rlung g.yab kyis g.yab gus pa'i mig gzir cing / /
man dA ra ba'i me tog rnams kyis yang dag 'thor / /
de bzhin gshegs pa bltams pa'i yon tan gyis tshim pa'i / /
gtsang mar lhag par gnas pa'i rnam dag sems can rnams / /
sdug bsngal nyid du bying ba'i 'gro la phan pa'i phyir / /
lha rnams 'dod chags bral ba na yang dga' bar gyur / /
gang gis rab tu bltams tshe ri rgyal phur pu nyid / /
rlung gis bsnun pa'i gru ltar sa gzhi g.yos gyur zhing / /
tsan+dan dang bcas ut+pal pad+ma'i snying po yi / /
char pa dag ni nam mkha'i sprin dang bral las babs / /
yid 'ong reg na bde ba'i rlung dag byung gyur te / /
lha yi na bza' dag ni mngon par 'bebs byed cing / /
nyi ma de nyid lhag par mngon par gsal ba ste / /
zhi ba'i 'od zer 'dus ma byas pa'i me 'bar ro / /
shar dang byang gi mtshams kyi khang pa'i phyogs gcig na / /
bsil ba'i chu yi khron pa rang byung gyur pa ste / /
pho brang btsun mo'i 'khor rnams ya mtshan gyur rnams kyis / /
gang la bya ba rnams ni stegs bzhin rab tu byas / /
chos dang ldan pa'i lha dang 'byung po'i tshogs rnams kyis / /
de ni lta ba'i don du nags tshal rab gang ste / /
rmad byung ngo mtshar gyur pa nyid kyi shing las kyang / /
me tog rnams ni dus ma yin par nges par brul / /
'tshe bar byed pa'i sems can rnams kyang de yi tshe / /
phan tshun dag tu phyin te gnod pa mi byed la / /
'tsho ba'i 'jig rten dag na nad gang ji snyed pa / /
de dag rnams kyang 'bad pa med par de tshe bcom / /
mkha' 'gro'i bya ni mtho min sgra sgrogs ri dwags kyang / /
chu klung dag ni chu yang zhi bar bab gyur la / /
phyogs rnams rab snang dge ba'i nam mkha' rab mdzes shing / /
lha yi rnga rnams mkha' la rab tu grags par gyur / /
rgud par gyur la mgon ni nye bar thob nas bzhin / /
'jig rten dag kyang mchog tu rab zhi thob gyur la / /
'jig rten rnams kyi thar pa'i bla ma rab bltams tshe / /
'dod pa'i lha nyid kho na dga' ba med par gyur / /
shin tu ngo mtshar sras kyi skye ba mthong gyur nas / /
mi bdag brtan pa yin yang rnam par 'gyur nas song / /
rab dga' skyes pa nyid dang yid mi bde skyes te / /
brtse ba las ni mchi ma rnam pa gnyis byung ngo / /
mi ma yin pa'i sras po nyid kyi nus pa dang / /
ma yi rang bzhin kyang ni stobs chung nyid kyi phyir / /
grang dang dro ba'i chu dag 'dres pa'i chu klung bzhin / /
lha mo 'jigs pa dang ni dga' bas gang bar 'gyur / /
lhag ma spangs te 'jigs pa nyid ni shes byas nas / /
yid 'ong 'dod pa'i ched du rtogs pa ma yin pa'i / /
bud med rgan mo rnams kyis bde legs gyur byas shing / /
gtsang mar byas te lha rnams dag la phyag 'tshal lo / /
de yi mtshan nyid dag kyang shes shing thos gyur nas / /
spyod dang thos dang tshig la grags thob bram ze rnams / /
rnam rgyas zhal ni ya mtshan dga' ba yis gang ste / /
dga' dang 'jigs par gyur pa'i mi yi lha la smras / /
mi dag sa la bu ma gtogs pa'i khyad 'phags pa / /
gzhan gang cung zad 'dod min zhi ba de yi phyir / /
khyod kyi sgron ma 'di ni rigs kyi sgron ma ste / /
khyod nyid dga' bar mdzod cig dga' ston da ltar bgyi / /
de phyir brtan par rnam dpyod med par dgar mdzod dang / /
rigs ni nges pa nyid du mchog tu 'phel bar 'gyur / /
'di ni khyod kyi bu zhes skyes par gyur pa ste / /
'jig rten sdug bsngal dag gis mngon par bcom pa'i mgon / /
mchog gyur 'di la mchog gyur gser gyi 'od mnga' zhing / /
sgron ma'i 'od zer dag gis mtshan rnams gang gyur pas / /
de nyid rtogs par gyur pa'i thub par 'gyur ba'am / /
yang na mi bdag sa stengs 'khor los sgyur bar 'gyur / /
sa yi bdag po nyid la gal te dga' 'gyur na / /
stobs dang chos dag gis ni de'i tshe sa stengs su / /
rgyal po kun gyi thog tu 'di ni gnas 'gyur te / /
skar ma'i 'od rnams la ni nyi ma'i 'od bzhin no / /
de ni gal te thar bzhed nags su gshegs gyur na / /
mkhyen dang de nyid kyis ni de tshe sa stengs su / /
lugs kun zil gyis mnan nas 'di ni gnas 'gyur te / /
mtho ba kun la ri rab ri yi rgyal po bzhin / /
ji ltar lcags rnams la ni gser dag mchog yin la / /
ri rnams la ni ri rab chu bo rnams la mtsho / /
gza' rnams la ni zla ba gdung byed rnams la nyi / /
de ltar khyod kyi sras ni rkang gnyis rnams kyi mchog /
gang gi spyan dag mi 'dzums mig gzir rnam par spangs pa ste / /
brtan zhing shin tu ring la dkar min rdzi ma dang / /
gzi brjid ldan pa yin yang 'on kyang zhi ba nyid / /
'di ni kun nas gzigs pa'i spyan mnga' ci la min / /
de nas gnyis skyes rnams la mi bdag gis smras pa / /
bdag nyid chen po mi skyong snga mas ma mthong ba / /
mthong zhes khyad 'di gang yin 'di la rgyu mtshan ci / /
de nas bram ze rnams kyis de nyid la smras pa / /
blo dang thos pa las dang grags pa rnams la ni / /
mi skyong sngon dang phyi ma nyid ni tshad ma yin / /
dngos po'i lugs la 'dir ni bya ba rgyu yin la / /
'dir yang bdag gi dper brjod dag ni mkhyen par mdzod / /
gang zhig rgyal po'i bstan bcos shes ldan ngan spong dag /
rig byed drang srong de gnyis kyis ni ma byas pa / /
de dag gi sras zhi ba pa wa sangs dang ni / /
phur bu yis ni dus kyis de nyid bskyed par gyur / /
nyams gyur snga ma rnams kyis ma mthong rig byed gang / /
dbyangs can ma yi bu yis kyang ni slar smras pa / /
nus med gnas 'jog gis ni ma byas gyur pa gang / /
rgyas pa yis ni de ltar rnam pa mang por brjod / /
'pho byed drang srong chen pos ma bsdebs gyur pa gang / /
tshig gi rkang pa grog mkhar gyis ni dang por bskyed / /
gso ba gang yang rgyun shes kyis ni ma mthong ba / /
phyi nas de ni drang srong rgyun shes bu yis byas / /
gang yang gnyis skyes nyid ni kun shas ma rnyed pa / /
de ni gting dpogs bu yis rgyal po la thob bo / /
bu ram shing pas dang por ma bsdams gyur pa gang / /
rgya mtsho la ni dug bcas kyis kyang mtshams bzung ngo / /
slob dpon nyid du bram ze'i rnal 'byor cho ga la / /
gzhan rnams kyis ma thob pa skyed byed gshegs par gyur / /
khyab 'jug gi ni grags pa'i las rnams gang yin pa / /
de rnams la ni dpa' bo la sogs stobs med gyur / /
de phyir lang tsho dang ni rigs dag tshad ma yin / /
la la la lar mchog nyid nyer thob 'jig rten na / /
rgyal dang drang srong rnams kyis snga mas ma byas pa / /
de dang de dag rnams ni bu rnams dag gis byas / /
de ltar gnyis skyes de rnams kyis ni yid ches te / /
mi skyong dbugs 'byin dang yang mngon par dga' gyur la / /
mi 'dod the tshom dag ni yid las rnam bstsal te / /
rab tu dga' ba nyid la lhag par 'dzegs par gyur / /
dga' ba yis ni gnyis skyes dam pa de rnams la / /
bkur sti sngon du 'gro ba'i nor rnams rab phul te / /
ji skad smras bzhin 'di ni sa yi bdag por gyur / /
rgas pa thos nas nags rnams su ni 'gro bar shog /
de nas mtshan ma rnams dang dka' thub stobs las ni / /
skye ba mthar mdzad bltams pa de ni rtogs gyur nas / /
dam pa'i chos la gus pa'i shAkya'i dbang phyug gi /
gnas su dkar min drang srong chen por gshegs par gyur / /
tshangs pa'i dpal nyid kyis kyang dka' thub dpal gyis ni / /
'bar ba'i tshang rig rnams kyi tshang rig de la ni / /
rgyal po'i bla mas gus pa dang ni bkur sti'i phyir / /
mi dbang pho brang du ni rab tu spyan drangs so / /
de ni sa bdag btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nye logs su / /
gzhon nu bltams pa la ni dga' ba'i shugs kyis 'ongs / /
dka' thub mchog las dang ni rgas pa la brten nas / /
brtan pa nags kyi 'du shes kyis ltar rnam par zhugs / /
de nas thub pa gdan la gnas pa de la mi skyong gis / /
zhabs bsil mchod yon sngon 'gro yang dag rab mchod nas / /
sngon tshe gnas mchog la ni mtha' can lhas bzhin des / /
ji ltar nye bar spyod la snyan gsan phab pa'o / /
bdag gi rigs ni rjes su bzung phyir nor ldan des / /
gang zhig bdag la gzigs phyir bcom ldan nyer gshegs la / /
bka' drin gnang bar mdzod cig zhi ba ci bgyi bgyi / /
kho bo slob ma lags so thugs rjes mdzad par rigs / /
de ltar mi skyong gis ni dngos po thams cad kyis / /
nye bar gsol btab gyur pa'i thub pa ji lta bzhin / /
rab rgyas yangs pa'i spyan ni ya mtshan dang bcas pas / /
zab ba dang ni brtan pa'i chig rnams smras pa'o / /
chos 'dod gtong ba dang ldan 'gron la sdug cing phangs / /
bdag nyid chen po khyed la 'thad pa 'di yin la / /
sems pa rjes 'gro ye shes lang tsho rjes mthun pa / /
khyod kyi blo gros gnyen gang de ltar bdag la yin / /
de dang de ni gang gis mi skyong drang srong des / /
phra mo'i chos kyi nor rnams rab tu thob byas nas / /
rtag par cho ga bzhin du mchod sbyin byas gyur pa / /
dka' thub rnams kyis phyug cing nor rnams dag gis dbul / /
bdag gi nye bar 'ongs la dgos pa gang yin pa / /
bdag gi de ni gson mdzod dga' bar nyer song khyed / /
byang chub rtogs pa'i ched du khyod kyi sras bltams zhes / /
lha yi ngag dag bdag gi nyi ma'i lam du thos / /
ngag de thos nas dang ni yid la bsgoms nas dang / /
mtshan ma rnams kyis shes nas de nas nye bar 'ongs / /
brgya byin gyi ni rgyal mtshan yang dag bsgreng ba bzhin / /
shAkya'i rigs kyi rgyal mtshan blta bar 'dod pa yis / /
zhes pa'i tshig 'di de ltar thos par gyur nas ni / /
mi dbang rab tu dga' bas kun nas g.yos gyur te / /
yum gyi pang du son las gzhon nu blangs nas ni / /
dka' thub nor can la ni yang dag bstan par gyur / /
de nas drang srong che des zhabs la 'khor los mtshan / /
phyag dang zhabs kyi sor mo dra bas 'brel ba dang / /
glang po bzhin du mdoms nub smin ma mdzod spur bcas / /
ya mtshan dang bcas rgyal po'i sras ni mthong bar gyur / /
lha mo'i pang na zhugs pa me yi bu bzhin du / /
ma ma'i pang du bzhugs pa mngon par mthong nas ni / /
byung gyur rdzi ma'i mtha' ru mchi ma rnams byung ste / /
dbugs med gyur nas gyen du lta la zhal phyogs gyur / /
mig dag mchi mas yongs gang dkar min mthong nas ni / /
bu la brtse ba'i phyir ni mi skyong 'dar gyur te / /
mchi ma dang ni gre ba kha zhing ldab ldib bcas / /
thal mo sbyar zhing yan lag btud de dris par gyur / /
gang gi lus ni lha las bar na cung zad cig /
rang gi skye ba ngo mtshar mang po'i sgron ma ste / /
gang gi don ni mchog tu 'gyur bar smra ba ste / /
rab tu mthong nas brtan pa gang phyir mchi ma 'ong / /
bcom ldan gzhon nu brtan pa'i tshe can yin snyam mam / /
bdag gi mya ngan ched du skyes pa min nam ci / /
bdag la chu yi snyim pa ci zhig ltar rnyed de / /
'di ni dus kyis 'thung phyir nye bar 'ongs ma yin / /
bdag gi snyan grags gter ni mi zad yin snyam mam / /
nges par bdag gi rigs kyi lag nor yin snyam ci / /
bde bar pha rol du ni rab tu 'gro snyam mam / /
gnyid par gyur kyang bu ni phye ba'i mig gcig yod / /
bdag gi rigs kyi myu gu skyes pa ma rgyas par / /
yongs su skams pa'i skal ba can zhig min snyam mam / /
khyab bdag myur bar gsungs shig bdag la zhi ba med / /
gnyen 'dun rnams kyis bu la brtse ba khyed kyis rig /
de ltar mi 'dod blo yis 'khrul ba byung gyur pa / /
rig nas mi dbang rgyal la thub pa des smras pa / /
bdag gis smras pa gang de the tshom med pa de / /
mi skyong khyed kyi blo gros gzhan gang ma gyur cig /
'di yi gzhan gyur mtshon min bdag gi rnam 'gyur te / /
'on kyang rang la slu bar rab mtshon rnam par 'khrugs / /
skye ba zad pa'i rnyed par bla min rtogs pa po / /
'di skyes bdag gi 'gro ba la ni dus yin no / /
rgyal srid rnam par spangs nas yul rnams la mi gnas / /
'bad pa drag po rnams kyis de nyid thob byas nas / /
'di ni 'gro la gti mug mun pa rnam 'joms phyir / /
ye shes rang bzhin nyi ma rab tu 'bar bar 'gyur / /
sdug bsngal rgya mtsho nad rnams bkram pa'i dbu ba can / /
rga ba'i dba' rlabs 'chi ba'i shugs ni drag po las / /
'gro ba nyam thag bying bar gyur rnams 'di yis ni / /
ye shes gru bo chen po yis ni sgrol bar byed / /
shes rab chu yi shugs la brten pa'i tshul khrims ngogs / /
ting nge 'dzin ni bsil ba'i brtul zhugs ngang pa 'phyo / /
'di yi mchog gi chos kyi chu bos rab bskor la / /
sred pas nyam thag gson pa'i 'jig rten 'thung bar byed / /
sdug bsngal gyis nyam thag dang yul gyis bsgribs rnams dang / /
'khor ba'i 'brog dgon 'jigs par gnas pa rnams la ni / /
lam rab chud zos rnams la lam 'gro rnams bzhin du / /
'dis ni rnam par dag pa'i lam dag 'chad par 'gyur / /
yul gyi bud shing can gyi 'dod chags me yis ni / /
'jig rten skye bo rnam par bsregs par gyur pa la / /
sos ka'i tha mar sprin chen gyis ni char bzhin du / /
'di yi chos kyi char gyis rab tu sim byed 'gyur / /
sred pa'i sgo gtan ma rig mun pa'i sgo glegs can / /
sgo la skye dgu rnams kyi 'thon pa'i rgyu las ni / /
'di yis mchog rab kun nas rnyed par dka' ba yi / /
dam pa'i chos kyi sgras ni rnam par 'byed par 'gyur / /
rang gi las kyi zhags pa rnams kyis yongs dkris shing / /
sdug bsngal dag gis mngon par zil non rten med pa'i / /
'jig rten rnams kyi rdzogs pa'i byang chub brnyes nas kyang / /
chos kyi rgyal po 'dis ni 'ching ba mthar mdzad 'gyur / /
rmongs sam 'dod pa'i bde ba yis sam rgyags las rung / /
'di yi mthar thug chos gang thos par mi byed pa / /
mi yi 'jig rten 'dir de mya ngan bya ba'i gnas / /
de phyir khyed nyid 'di la mya ngan ma byed cig /
yon tan rgya mtsho 'di las 'khrul gyur bdag gi ni / /
bsam gtan rnams ni thob kyang don byas med nyid de / /
de yi dam chos ma thos pa la kho bo ni / /
mtho ris dag na gnas kyang phun tshogs med pa snyam / /
de ltar don thos bshes dang bcas shing btsun mor bcas / /
yid mi bde ba dor nas mi dbang dgar gyur la / /
rnam pa de ltar bdag gi bu ni 'di'o zhes / /
des ni bdag nyid la ni snying bo ldan par bsams / /
'phags pa'i chos rnams kyis kyang 'gro bar 'gyur ro zhes / /
bsam pa'i rnam par gzung bya snying la byas gyur te / /
nges par 'di ni mi sdug chos kyi phyogs min la / /
rigs rgyud nyams pa las ni 'on kyang 'jigs pa mthong / /
de nas bu la rnam par 'khrugs pa'i rgyal po la / /
bu yi nges pa'i de nyid rig par byas nas su / /
gus bcas gyen du gzugs mthong dkar min thub pa ni / /
rlung gi lam gyis ji ltar 'ongs par gshegs par gyur / /
blo gros byas pa'i sring mo'i bu yang mthong nas ni / /
thub pa'i gsung mnyan pa dang de yi lugs la ni / /
rnam mang rjes su brtse ba yis ni legs pa des / /
sdug pa'i bu bzhin du ni sbyor ba byed du bcug /
sras po skyes pas tshim pa'i mi yi bdag po yang / /
yul la song ba'i 'ching ba rnams ni rnam spangs te / /
sras kyi yid 'ong sras po bltams pa'i las dag ni / /
rigs dang 'dra bar ji lta ba bzhin byed du bcug /
zhag bcu yongs su 'das par gyur ba nyid kyi tshe / /
mchog gi dga' ba rab ldan snyoms par gyur pa'i yid / /
sras las mchog tu 'gyur phyir lha yi mchod pa ni / /
bzlas brjod dang ni sbyin sreg bkra shis la sogs byas / /
gzhan yang brgya dang stong phrag yongs su gang ba'i grangs / /
brtan dang stobs ldan bu rnams gser gyi rwar bcas shing / /
rgas pa nye bar 'ongs min swa ma ldan pa'i ba / /
rang gi sras 'phel phyir na gnyis skyes rnams la byin / /
de nas snyoms pa'i bdag nyid kyis ni rnam mang yul / /
rang sems tshim bar byed pa'i bya ba rnams byas nas / /
yon tan ldan zhing dge ba'i yud tsam nges pa na / /
grong khyer rab tu 'jug la dga' bas blo gros mdzad / /
de nas mche gnyis mche ba las byung rin thang che / /
dkar po'i me tog gis spras nor bu'i sgron / /
khri la dge ba'i phyir ni lha mo sras ldan ma / /
lha rnams la ni rab tu btud nas bsnyen par gyur / /
de nas gnas brtan skye mo rjes 'brang sras mgon ma / /
bdag po ldan ma grong la mdun du rab zhugs nas / /
mchod ldan lha na lha rnams kyis ni brgya byin bzhin / /
mi bdag nyid kyang grong ba'i tshogs kyis gshegs par gyur / /
de nas gdong drug skyes pas yid ches dbang phyug bzhin / /
shAkya'i rgyal pos grong khyer rnam par khyab mdzad de / /
zhal ni dga' bas rab gang 'di dang 'di zhes pa'i / /
srid 'phel rgyas pa dang ni grags dang snyan pa mdzad / /
de nas mi yi bdag po'i sras bltams cher skyes pas / /
ser skya zhes pa'i grong khyer ljongs dang bcas pa de / /
gnod sbyin grong na phun tshogs 'dod ba skyes pa na / /
lha yi bu mo rnams kyis bkram bzhin dga' bar gyur / /
sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las /
gzhon nu sku bltams pa'i le'u ste dang po'o // //
skye dang rga ba mthong song bdag skyes bdag pham de'i / /
skyes pa nas brtsams mi nyid nyi mas rgyal po de / /
chu yi shugs rnams kyis ni chu bo sin d+hu bzhin / /
nor dang glang po rta dang bshes rnams 'phel bar gyur / /
nor rnams dang ni rin po che dang bzang po'i gser / /
de dang de ni byas dang ma byas pa nyid kyang / /
yid la re ba yi rang bzhin du khur gyur pa / /
de la gcig tu phan pa'i cha shas gter rnyed gyur / /
gang zhig pad+ma dang mtshungs gnyis 'thung rnams kyis kyang / /
dkyil 'khor 'di la nye bar 'ong bar mi nus pa'i / /
gangs dang ldan pa'i glang chen chang gis dregs de rnams / /
'bad pa las kyang gzhan du de la nye bar gnas / /
sna tshogs mtshan mas mtshan zhing gsar ba'i gser sga dang / /
de bzhin gzhan rnams dag gis brgyan byas rngog ma 'phyang / /
stobs dang byams pa dang ni nor gyis thob pa yi / /
'di yi mgyogs 'gro rnams kyis grong khyer phye mar byas / /
de bzhin 'di yi yul 'khor du ni tshim dang rgyas / /
legs la rdul ldan yon tan ldan pa 'o mar ldan / /
rab mchog be'u rnams dang bcas pa'i ba rnams ni / /
'o ma mang po 'jo ba mang po byung bar gyur / /
'di yi dgra bo dbus gnas nyid du song gyur pa / /
dbus gnas gyur pa mdza' bshes nyid du rab tu song / /
khyad par du ni bshes gnyen brtan por song ba ste / /
'di yi phyogs dag gnyis te dgra yang yod ma yin / /
de bzhin du ni 'di yi 'jam rlung 'brug gi sgra / /
glog gi phreng ba 'khyil ba yis ni brgyan pa'i sprin / /
rdo char dang ni thog lhung nyes pa rnams kyis gzhan / /
yul du dus la lha yis char pa phab par gyur / /
zhing gi las kyis ngal dub byed pa nyung ngus kyang / /
'bru ni 'bras bu ldan pa dus sbyor bzhin skyes te / /
de rnams nyid kyang 'di yi sman du byung gyur la / /
bcud dang snying po yis kyang mngon par lhags pa nyid / /
g.yul du rab tu zhugs la kun du 'joms pa bzhin / /
lus la the tshom za bar byed pa'i dus na yang / /
rang bzhin gnas shing bde ba nyid du nad med par / /
dus kyi dbang gis mi mo rnams ni rab tu btsas / /
brtul zhugs ldan rnams ma gtogs nor rdzas dman na yang / /
mi rnams pha rol rnams las don du gnyer mi byed / /
mngon par don du gnyer la 'phags pa nor 'phra yang / /
de tshe 'ga' zhig dag ni rgyab kyis phyogs ma gyur / /
de tshe rgyal po de yi rgyal srid la ni dga' / /
gnyen la zhe sa med min mi ster ba yang med / /
brtul zhugs med pa nyid min brdzun med 'tshe med pa / /
sgra mi bsgrags kyi sras po lta bu byung bar gyur / /
der yang skyed mos tshal dang lha gnas dka' thub gnas / /
khron pa rdzing dang dge bcu 'du ba'i gnas rnams kyi / /
bya ba rnams ni mtho ris bzhin du nyer thob nas / /
chos 'dod rnams kyis mngon sum du ni rab tu mdzad / /
mu ge dang ni 'jigs dang nad rnams las grol zhing / /
dgar gyur skye bo mtho ris gzhan du mngon par dga' / /
bdag mos bdag po la 'am mo yis bdag por rung / /
phan tshun log par mngon par spyod pa dag kyang med / /
dga' ba'i ched du 'dod la 'ga' zhig gis ma bsnyen / /
'dod pa'i don du nor ni 'ga' zhig gis ma bsrungs / /
nor gyi don du chos la 'ga' zhig gis ma spyad / /
chos kyi don du 'tshe ba 'ga' zhig gis ma byas / /
rkun po sogs dang dgra yang nyams par rang gnas med / /
pha rol mya ngan med pa ji lta ba nyid bzhin / /
rang gi 'khor lo pha rol 'khor lo las grol te / /
rgyal po de la bde dang lo legs byung bar gyur / /
de yi tshe na rgyal po de yi rgyal srid la / /
de skyes pa na nyi ma'i sras po'i yid shes bzhin / /
dga' bar spyad par gyur la sdig pa rab nyams shing / /
chos rnams 'bar zhing nyon mongs rnams ni zhi bar gyur / /
gang phyir rnam pa de ltar don kun grub pa dang / /
rgyal po'i rigs kyi phun sum tshogs pa byung gyur te / /
de phyir mi skyong gis ni sras po de yi mtshan / /
don kun grub pa zhes bya 'di ni rab tu mdzad / /
lha mo sgyu ma yang ni lha yi drang srong mtshungs / /
bu yi nus mthu rnam par spangs pa mthong nas ni / /
bltams la rab tu dga' mas bzod par ma nus te / /
de nas gnas pa'i ched du ltar ni gshegs par gyur / /
de nas lha yi mngal dang mtshungs pa'i gzhon nu la / /
byams pa'i rang bzhin gyis kyang khyad par med pa yi / /
ma yi nu mo mdangs mnyam pa yi rang bzhin la / /
yang dag skyed btsud bdag las skyes pa lta bur gyur / /
de nas nyi ma gzhon nu 'char rir gnas 'dra dang / /
rlung gis rab tu bus par gyur pa'i me bzhin dang / /
skar ma'i bdag po mun min phyogs la gnas pa ltar / /
gzhon nu de ni rim gyis yang dag 'phel bar gyur / /
de nas rin thang chen po'i tsan+dan rnams dang ni / /
rin chen phreng ba sman gyi snying por bcas rnams dang / /
ri dwags rab tu sbyar ba'i gser gyi shing rta rnams / /
'di yi ched du gshegs kyi khyim rnams dag nas blangs / /
lang tsho nyid dang rjes su mthun pa'i rgyan rnams dang / /
gser gyi rang bzhin ri dgas glang chen rta rnams dang / /
gser dang dngul gyis bris pa'i mi chung gzugs rnams dang / /
shing rta ba glang byung dus yang dag sbyar rnams blangs / /
de ni lang tsho rjes mthun yul la nye spyod pa / /
de rnams kyis ni yul la nyer spyad la / /
dpa' dang brtan pa yis dang blo dang dpal gyis kyang / /
byis pa yin yang byis min rab mtshungs byung bar gyur / /
lang tsho gzhon nu shin tu 'das nas yang dag par / /
'du byed las ni rab tu thob nas dus su ni / /
lo mang dag gis rtogs bya nyin zhag nyung ngu yis / /
rang dang rjes su mthun pa'i rigs pa rnams ni blangs / /
drang srong chen po dkar min las ni sngon rol du / /
de yi nyes legs don gyi skal ba thob nas ni / /
nags su gshegs par 'gyur zhes shAkya'i rgyal po yis / /
'dod pa rnams la chags pa skyed du bcug par gyur / /
brtan pa'i tshul khrims spyod pa can gyi rigs de la / /
ngo tsha dang ni dul ba nyer ldan legs ldan ma / /
grags 'dzin ma zhes grags pa rnam par yangs pa ma / /
btsun mor mngon par brjod pa'i dpal mo 'di la blangs / /
kun 'gyed gzhon nu dang ni rab tu mtshungs pa yis / /
mchog gi lus kyis snang zhing gsal ba de nyid ni / /
shAkya'i rgyal po'i mna' ma de dang thabs cig tu / /
bde sogs ma dang mig stong ldan bzhin mngon par dga' / /
yid kyang dpyod par byed la cung zhig rab log pa / /
gang gis mthong mi 'gyur zhes rjes su bsams byas nas / /
sa la rab tu spyod min lding khang lto nyid du / /
gnas dag mi skyong gis ni de la rnam par bstan / /
de nas gzhal med nam mkhar sa la spyod pa bzhin / /
ston kha'i dus kyi chu gter sprin ni dkar po yi / /
dus sbyor kun du bde ba'i gzhi yi lding khang la / /
bud med rnams kyi sil snyan rgya chen rnams kyis rnam par gshegs / /
gser gyis gdams pa'i rnga shing can gyi rdza rnga'i skad / /
mi mo'i lag pa'i rtse mos mngon par brdungs pa yi / /
lha mchog ma yi gar dang mnyam pa'i gar rnams kyis / /
ti se'i gangs ltar de yi pho brang mdzes par gyur / /
ngag dang gzo dang rol dang rnam 'gyur rnams kyis kyang / /
rgyags dang rtse dang dgod pa dngar mo rnams kyis dang / /
smin ma bskyod pa yis dang phyed mig lta rnams kyis / /
de la der ni mi mo rnams ni dga' bar gyur / /
de nas de ni 'dod pa bsten par mkhas pa yi / /
dga' bas dregs pa'i bud med rnams kyis bzung gyur la / /
gzhal med khang ni rgyab nas bsod nams las can bzhin / /
gzhal med khang ni rgyab nas sa la ma gshegs so / /
mi skyong gis kyang de nyid bskyed pa'i ched las ni / /
de yi 'byung bar 'gyur ba'i don gyis bskul gyur te / /
sdig pa las ni dga' bral zhi la mngon dga' zhing / /
legs la skal bar bgos shing dul la bsnyen par gyur / /
brtan min bzhin du 'dod pa'i bde la ma zhen la / /
ma rungs skyed ma la ni yang dag chags ma gyur / /
brtan pas dbang po'i rta ni stobs las rnam thul zhing / /
gnyen dang grong khyer pa rnams yon tan rnams kyis rgyal / /
gzhan gyi sdug bsngal phyir ni rig pa ma brjod la / /
ye shes dge ba gang yang de la lhag par brjod / /
des ni rang gi skye dgu rnams la ji lta bar / /
de ltar skye dgu rnams la dge ba'i bsngags pa mdzad / /
skar ma rgyal snang shes ldan sras po lhag pa'i lha / /
ji lta bar ni de yi tshe ring phyir mchod des / /
chung min me la bsreg bya rnams ni bsregs gyur la / /
gnyis skyes rnams la gser dang ba lang rnams kyang byin / /
'gram stegs chab rnams kyis dang yon tan chab rnams kyis / /
gtsang sbra'i ched du lus dang yid la khrus byas te / /
rig byed du ni nye bar bstan pa'i chang rnams dang / /
zhi ba bdag skyes snying la zhi ba'i bde la 'thung / /
gang zhig don dang mi ldan zhi ba ma smras la / /
gang zhig dga' ba dang bral de nyid ma brjod de / /
zhi ba de nyid med dang rtsub pa'i de nyid phyir / /
ngo tsha ba yis bdag nyid kho na brjod ma nus / /
don ldan 'dod pa rnams dang mi 'dod pa rnams la / /
chags pa'i skyon la brten nas rab tu 'thob min te / /
dge ba'i tha snyad gtsang ma la ni bsnyen gyur la / /
mchod sbyin la yang ma mos de ltar ji lta bzhin / /
sred pa dang ldan mngon par 'ongs pa de ma thag /
sbyin bya chu 'dra rnams kyis skom pa bcad gyur la / /
g.yul las ma gtogs ye shes kyi ni sta ri yis / /
dgra bo rnams kyi nga rgyal chen po bcom par gyur / /
gcig ni rnam par dul la des ni mdun bsrungs shing / /
bdun po nyid ni don la lnga po dag ni bsrungs / /
sde tshan gsum po thob la sde tshan gsum rtogs shing / /
sde tshan gnyis po shes la sde tshan gnyis po spangs / /
nyes pa byas kyang rab tu bskyangs nas gzhom bya la / /
'tshe bar mi byed khro bas kyang ni gzigs ma yin / /
de rnams dag la 'bras bu zhi bas bcings gyur la / /
de rnams dag ni 'dor ba tshul ma yin phyir mthong / /
drang srong rnams kyis mchog gi brtul zhugs spyad gyur la / /
yun rings yang dag bzung ba'i sha khon zhugs rnams dor / /
yon tan dri ldan snyan dngags rnams ni thob gyur la / /
dri ma can du byed pa'i rdul rnams rnam par dor / /
rab tu mi gnas gtor ma'i dpya ni ma blangs la / /
pha rol dngos po rnams la mngon par rlom ma byas / /
dgra rnams la ni chos ma yin pa ma smras la / /
khro ba rnams ni snying gis gzung ba ma yin no / /

rnal 'byor rab tu ldan pa'i dbang po rnams ci ltar / /
der ni de ltar sa bdag rab tu sgyur ba can / /
'bangs dang grong khyer ba rnams de lta nyid du byas / /
de nas mdzes pa'i 'o ma 'dzin pa dang ldan ma / /
grags 'dzin ma ni rang gi grags pa 'dzin ma la / /
zas gtsang sras po'i sras po sgra gcan sgra yi zhal / /
sgra gcan 'dzin zhes bya ba dus su skyes par gyur / /
de nas 'dod pa'i bu mnga' mchog gi yid ches te / /
rigs rgyud 'phel ba rab mtshon sa skyong rgyal po ni / /
ji lta nyid du sras po rab tu skyes la dga' / /
de lta nyid du sras po'i sras po skyes la dga' / /
bdag gi bu yi bur gyur pa la brtse ba ni / /
bdag bzhin gang las yin zhes dga' ba skyes gyur te / /
dus su des ni cho ga de dang de dmigs shing / /
bu la dga' ba mtho ris bzhin du 'dzegs par gyur / /
rgyal po'i khyu mchog grags dang snyan pas mtshan rnams kyis / /
dang po'i skal ba rnams kyi lam la gnas nas ni / /
dkar po ma dor dka' thub rnams la dka' thub dang / /
'tshe ba dor ba'i mchod sbyin rnams kyis mchod par gyur / /
rgyal po'i dpal gyis dang ni dka' thub dpal gyis kyang / /
bsod nams las can de ni de nas 'bar gyur la / /
rigs dang blo dang mdzad spyod kyis kyang gsal ba ste / /
gzi brjid stong gi 'od zer bzhin du rab tu 'phro / /
rang byung las byung mchod byed sngags ni mchod byas nas / /
sras gnas ched du brtan pa'i dpal gyis bzlas byas shing / /
dka' thub byed pa'i las rnams byas gyur skye dgu rnams / /
skyed 'dod skye dgu'i bdag bzhin dang po'i dus su'o / /
mtshon cha spangs shing bstan bcos rnam par shes gyur la / /
nye bar zhi la bsnyen zhing nges la rnam par bzod / /
dbang ldan bzhin du yul rnams gang la ma bsnyen la / /
yab mes bzhin du yul rnams kun la gzigs par gyur / /
des kyang bu yi ched du rgyal srid bzung gyur la / /
bu ni rigs kyi don du rigs ni grags pa'i phyir / /
grags pa mtho ris ched du mtho ris bdag nyid phyir / /
chos kyi don du bdag nyid gnas la 'dod par 'gyur / /
de ltar des ni dam pa rnams kyis nges thob pa'i / /
thos pa las grub chos ni rnam pa sna tshogs byas / /
gang las bdag gi bus ni bu yi ngo mthong nas / /
nags tshal nyid du 'gro mi 'gyur zhes mgon bslangs so / /

sa skyong rnams kyis sa la bu ni bsrung ba ste / /
chos ni 'dod pa'i ma yi dbang po de yis kyang / /
yul rnams 'dor ba med par bu ni chos las bsrungs / /
byang chub sems dpa' yul la bde ba'i ro shes thams cad kyang / /

de phyir nye bar bsags pa'i las ni rtsa nas skyed pa'i phyir / /
de ni zhi ba ma thob de srid dga' ba bsnyen par gyur / /
sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las /
btsun mo'i 'khor na gnas pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o // //
de nas re zhig dus na 'jam po'i rtswa rnams dang / /
khu byug pho ni gyen du skad 'don rkang 'thung rnams / /
glu rnams dang ni nges ldan skyed mos tshal rnams ni / /
pad+ma'i 'byung gnas kyis brgyan des ni thos par gyur / /
de nas bud med skye bo rnams ni dga' ba yi / /
grong khyer skyed mos tshal gyi yid 'ong dngos thos te / /
khyim gyi nang du mngon par bkag pa'i glu bzhin du / /
phyi rol rab tu 'gro ba'i ched du blo mdzad do / /
de nas sras su mngon brjod yid 'ong de yi ni / /
dgongs pa mi skyong gis ni nges par thos gyur nas / /

ltad mo dag la rnam par gshegs par bka' stsal to / /

'khogs pa nad pa la sogs bkren rnams phyogs rnams su / /

rgyal po'i lam rnams dag ni mchog tu mdzes par byas / /
de nas dpal ldan rgyal po'i lam ni byas pa na / /
dpal ldan rnam par dul ba rjes 'brangs gzhon nu ni / /
gzhal yas khang pa'i logs nas dus su mngon babs nas / /
mngon par rjes gnang byas pa mi skyong la mngon gshegs / /
de nas mi dbang bu la mchi ma byung gyur te / /
mgo la nye bar bsnams te yun rings rnam gzigs nas / /
song cig ces ni tshig gi bka' dag stsal gyur la / /
brtse ba dag las de ni yid kyis ma btang ngo / /
de nas de ni 'dzam bu chu gser sga 'dzin pa'i / /
legs par bslabs pa'i mgyogs 'gro bzhi yis sbyar ba yi / /

de nas 'bras spos me tog 'bar ba rab bkram zhing / /
phreng ba rnam dpyangs rab tu g.yo ba'i ba dan can / /
zla ba skar ma dang bcas bar snang la bzhin du / /
'dra ba rjes 'brang lam ni rab tu thob par gyur / /
ya mtshan gyur las rab tu rgyas pa'i mig rnams ni / /
ut+pal sngon po'i phyed 'dra rnams kyis bkram pa ni / /
rgyal po'i lam la dal bu dal bus gshegs gyur te / /

kha cig dag ni 'di la mngon du phyogs nas kyang / /
dpal dang tshe yi rnam par rgyas la shis pa brjod / /

tshogs pa rnams ni rigs chen rnams la nges dral nas / /

skyen por 'gro bar nus pa yin yang gzhan ma yin / /

phan tshun rab tu bcer bas ril por gyur pa rnams / /
yang dag drud las bskyod gyur rna lung 'khyil ba can / /
de dag rnams kyi de tshe sgra bcas rgyan rnams ni / /
rlung bgrod skar khung rnams su rab tu zhi bar gyur / /
rlung bgrod skar khung rnams las rnam par 'thon pa rnams / /
phan tshun thang chen gyur pa'i rna lung 'khyil ba rnams / /
bud med rnams kyi 'dam skyes 'dra ba'i 'dam skyes zhal / /
lding khang rnams su bkod pa rnams ni rnam par mdzes / /
de nas khang bzangs lang tsho ma rnams kyis khyab cing / /
ya mtshan la ni rab phye skar khung rnams kyis ni / /
lha mo dang bcas gzhal med rnams kyi nam mkha' bzhin / /
dpal dang ldan pa'i grong khyer kun nas mdzes par gyur / /
skar khung rnams kyis rnam par yangs pa ma yin las / /
phan tshun 'gram par bkod pa'i rna lung can rnams kyis / /
'dam skyes pad+ma rnams kyi tshogs rnams bcings pa bzhin / /

gyen du gdong phyogs de la rab tu lta ba yi / /
mi rnams gnam la 'gro bar 'dod bzhin mdzes par gyur / /
lus dad dpal gyis mchog tu 'bar bar gyur pa yi / /
rgyal po'i sras de mthong nas bud med de rnams ni / /
nges par dgongs pa gzhan min bsam pa dag pa yis / /
'di yi chung ma skal ba bzang zhes dal bus smra / /
gzugs kyi dngos su me tog tog can dang mtshungs shing / /
rnam par ring zhing rgyas pa'i dpung pa can 'di ni / /
dpal nyid dor nas chos la nye bar gshegs zhes te / /
de la de dag rnams kyis zhe sa kho na byas / /
rnam par dul la gtsang zhing brtan pa'i cha lugs can / /
grong pa rnams kyis de ltar rgyal po'i lam khyab pa / /
de ni sngon du gzhon nus mthong nas dga' bas te / /
bdag gi srid pa gzhan ma cung zhig brtags pa 'dra / /
grong khyer de yang mtho ris bzhin du rab dga' ba / /
mngon par gzigs nas gtsang mar gnas pa'i lha rnams kyis / /
sa gzhi skyong ba'i sras po yang dag bskul don du / /
'khogs pa'i mi rgan rab tu 'gro bar sprul gyur to / /
de nas gzhon nu yis ni rga bas zil non zhing / /
mi rnams las ni tha dad dbyibs can de gzigs nas / /
g.yo ba med cing de nyid du ni zhugs pa'i spyan / /
chags par gyur cing kha lo 'dzin pa la smras so / /
mngon par nyer 'ongs mi de su yin 'dren pa kye / /
skra rnams dkar zhing dbyug pa la ni lag pas brten / /
smin mas kun nas mig g.yogs 'khogs shing yan lag drud / /
rnam 'gyur 'di ni tha mal gang 'dod yin nam ci / /
de skad ces smra shing rta rab tu 'dren pa po / /
lha mchog de rnams nyid kyi blo ni rmongs byas shing / /
don ni bsrung bya yin yang skyon med mthong gyur te / /
de yis sa skyong bdag nyid skyes la nges par gsol / /
gzugs kyi gnod byed stobs kyi rnam par za ba po / /
rgan pa rnams kyi 'joms byed mya ngan rnams kyi sa / /
dran pa rnams kyi nyams byed dbang po rnams kyi dgra / /
'di ni rgas pa zhes bya gang gis 'di bcom mo / /
'dis kyang byis pa nyid dang 'o ma 'thung gyur cing / /
dus kyi sa la yongs su gnyid log gyur pa ste / /
rim gyis lus rab ldan pa'i lang tshor gyur nas kyang / /
rim gyis de nyid kho nas rga bar nye bar song / /
de skad ces smras rgyal po'i bdag nyid skyes pa ste / /
cung zhig 'dar la kha lo sgyur la 'di skad smras / /
skyon 'di kho bo la yang 'byung ba min nam ci / /
de bzhin 'di la kha lo sgyur ba yis gsol to / /
'di ni na tshod rab mchog tshe dang ldan pa'i yang / /
gdon mi za bar dus kyi dbang gis 'byung bar 'gyur / /
de bzhin rgas pa gzugs kyi rnam par nyams pa bor / /
'jig rten pa yi shes pa nyid dang mthong ba nyid / /
de nas sngon gyi bsam pa dag pa'i blo mnga' ba / /
rnam rgyas bskal par bsags pa'i bsod nams las can de / /
rdo rje chen po'i sgra la nye bar ba lang bzhin / /
rgas pa thos nas gzhon nu kun nas yi mug gyur / /
dbugs ni ring du brgyus nas rang gi mgo bsgul zhing / /
'khogs pa de la spyan ni rnam par zhugs nas su / /
rga ba dang bcas skye ba de rnams gzigs gyur nas / /
sems ni khong du chud pa de yis tshig 'di smras / /
dran pa dang ni gzugs dang pha rol gnon pa yang / /
de ltar rgas pas rnam dpyod med par 'joms pas te / /
'di lta bur ni mngon sum nyid du song na yang / /
'jig rten pa dag skyo med nyer 'gro kho na'o / /
de ltar song la 'dren pa rta rnams phyir zlog la / /
khyod ni khyim nyid du ni skyes par rab tu song / /
rgas pa'i 'jigs pa'i sems su gnas pa kho bo la / /
skyed mos tshal gyi sa la bde ba ga la yod / /
de nas rgyal po'i sras po de yi bka' lung gis / /
kha lo sgyur bas shing rta phyir la bzlog par gyur / /
de nas gzhon nus pho brang de nyid kho nar ni / /
bsam pa'i dbang gis stong pa bzhin du rab tu thob / /
gang gi tshe na de yang bde ba ma yin te / /
rgas pa rgas pa zhes ni rab tu yongs su rtog /
de nas mi dbang gis ni rjes gnang de ni slar / /
rim gyis de nyid kho nas phyi rol gshegs par gyur / /
de nas gzhan yang lus la nad dang yongs ldan pa / /
lha mchog de rnams nyid kyis bskyed cing sprul pa'i mi / /
zas gtsang rgyal po'i sras po can der song nyid kyis / /
gzigs nas kha lo sgyur ba de nyid la smras pa / /
gsus pa sbom zhing dbugs dag skyod pa'i lus po can / /
lag pa cha shas zha zhing rid la skya bseng lus / /
a ma zhes ni snying rje'i ngag dag smra ba po / /
gzhan la brten nas gnas pa'i mi de su zhig yin / /
de nas kha lo sgyur bas smras pa zhi ba kye / /
'di yi khams ni rab 'khrugs rab stobs rab tu 'phel / /
nad ces bya ba mngon brjod shin tu don med chen po ste / /
nus kyang gang gis de ni rab dbang med par byas / /
rjes su brtse bcas mi de la ni gzigs bzhin du / /
rgyal po'i sras des slar yang 'di skad ces smras pa / /
skyes gyur skyon de so sor 'di nyid kho na'i 'am / /
nad kyi 'jigs la skye dgu rnams kyi spyi la yin / /
de nas shing rta rab tu 'dren pa des smras pa / /
gzhon nu nyes pa de ni thun mong gyur pa ste / /
de ltar nad rnams dag ni yongs su gtser ba ni / /
nad mthar phyin na 'jig rten dga' bar nye bar gshegs / /
de ltar don thos sems ni khong du chud pa de / /
chu rlabs nang song ri bong can bzhin rab 'dar zhing / /
brtse ba thugs rje mnga' bas gsung ngag tshig 'di ni / /
cung zhig dngar ba'i dbyangs kyis rab tu smras pa'o / /
skye dgu rnams la rnam par zhen pa'i nad 'di ni / /
'jig rten pa dag rang bzhin gnas shing blo gtad byed / /
mi shes rnam par rgya chen e ma mi rnams kyis / /
gang zhig nad las rnam par grol rnams bzhad gad byed / /
'dren pa phyi rol rab tu 'gro las phyir log la / /
mi dbang pho brang nyid du shing rta rab tu song / /
bdag gi nad kyi 'jigs pa thos nas dga' ba las / /
sems ni 'khums pa bzhin du rab tu bcom par gyur / /
de ltar lan gnyis phyir log de ni rab gzigs nas / /
sa yi bdag po yis kyang yongs su gros byas so / /
de yi phyir log nges pa'i mtshan ma thos gyur nas / /
bdag cag rnams ni 'di yis yang dag 'dor snyam ste / /
lam rnams gtsang mar lhag par byed pa po rnams la / /
khros shing 'khrugs kyang chad pa drag pos gcod pa med / /
slar yang sras po de la khyad par 'phags pa dang / /
ldan pa'i yul la rab tu dpyod pa rnams mdzad cing / /
dbang po g.yo ba nyid kyi phyir yang chags snyam ste / /
bdag cag rnam par mi 'dor zhes ni mgon blangs so / /
gang gi tshe na sgra sgrogs dbang po'i don rnams kyis / /
sras po 'di la pho brang 'khor na dga' ba med / /
de nas ro gzhan ro la gyur cig zhes sems shing / /
phyi rol ltad mo la ni rnam par bka' stsal to / /
brtse ba las ni sras po'i dgongs ba rtogs nas su / /
de la chags pa'i skyon rnams 'ga' zhig ma bsams nas / /
sgyu rtsal rnams la mngon par shes zhes res ma'i gtso / /
mdzangs ma rnams la des ni yang dag bka' stsal to / /
de nas khyad par du yang mi yi dbang po'i lam / /
legs par brgyan byas nyid dang yongs su brtags pa la / /
'dren pa dang ni shing rta brjes nas rgyal po yis / /
gzhon nu phyi rol du ni rab tu gshegs su gzhug /
de nas de ltar rgyal po'i bu ni gshegs pa na / /
lha mchog de rnams nyid kyis rnam par sprul pa yi / /
srog song shi ba'i ro de lam du bteg pa ni / /
'dren pa dang ni gzhon nus mthong ste gzhan gyis min / /
de nas 'dren pa rgyal po'i sras po des smras pa / /
zhan zhing stug pa'i mi rnams dag ni rjes 'brang zhing / /
rgyan gyis brgyan pa yin yang kun nas ngu ba ste / /
mi bzhi rnams kyis bteg pa pha gi su zhig yin / /
de nas gtsang ba'i bdag nyid gtsang mar gnas pa yi / /
lha rnams dag gis sems ni zil non 'dren pa po / /
nges ni brjod par bya ba min kyang don 'di ni / /
don ldan dbang phyug la ni rab tu rnam par gsol / /
blo dang dbang po srog gi yon tan dang bral zhing / /
gnyid log ming bral rtswa dang shing du gyur pa ste / /
brtson 'grus ldan pa rnams kyis bskyed nas bsrungs nas kyang / /
sdug pa sdug pa rnams kyis spangs pa de ni su yin nam / /
de ltar tshig ni rab tu 'dren pa las thos nas / /
cung zhig kun nas bskyod cing de nyid la smras pa / /
chos 'di nyid ni skye ba 'di nyid kyang gi'am / /
mthar gyur 'di 'dra skye dgu kun gyi yin nam ci / /
de nas rab tu 'dren pas 'di nyid la gsol pa / /
mthar gyur las 'di skye dgu rnams ni kun gyi ste / /
dman dang 'bring dang bdag nyid chen po thams cad kyi / /
'jig rten dag ni rnam par nges par rnam par nyams par 'gyur / /
de nas mi dbang sras po de ni bstan na yang / /
'chi ba thos nas de ma thag tu yi mug cing / /

gdangs snyan dang ldan dbyangs kyis rab tu smras pa'o / /
'di ni nges par skye dgu rnams kyi mthar thug ste / /
'jig rten pa dag 'jigs pa spangs shing bag med la / /
mi rnams dag gi sems rnams sra ba snyam pa ste / /
lam la gnas rnams de ltar rang bzhin nyid du gnas / /
de phyir 'dren pa shing rta'i kha ni phyir bzlog dang / /

mi bdag bdag skyes kyis ni de skad smras na yang / /
de yis shing rta de ni phyir la ma bzlog ste / /
khyab par ldan pa yin yang mi dbang brten pa la / /
pad+ma'i tshogs bcas nags nyid du ni gshegs par gyur / /
de nas me tog rgyas ldan gzhon nu'i rkang 'thung zhing / /
yongs su bskor zhing rab dga' myos pa'i khu byug can / /

yan lag mchog ma'i tshogs khyab mi skyong bdag skyes sras / /

de nas skyed mos tshal de nas / /
ya mtshan gyis ni mig g.yos rnams / /
bud med rnams ni khyo thob bzhin / /

'ongs nas de la de rnams kyis / /
ya mtshan rab rgyas spyan ma drangs / /
pad+ma'i mdzod 'dra'i phyag rnams kyis / /

yid dkrugs 'dod pas sems g.yengs rnams / /

khyod la grogs su nus pa lo / /
gang phyir khyed la smra 'dod pa / /
rab dga' ldan pa de phyir ro / /
phan pa min las rab 'gegs shing / /
phan pa la yang rjes rab 'jug /
sdug pa na yang yongs mi gtong / /
yongs rdzogs shes kyi mtshan nyid do / /
bdag de byams par dam bcas nas / /
skyes bu'i don la phyir phyogs pa / /
gal te khyod la btang snyoms byed / /
grogs po nyid kyang ma yin no / /
de phyir mdza' bor gyur nas smras / /
gzhon nu'i lus dang ldan pa ni / /
khyod kyis 'di 'dra bud med kyis / /
yul la mkhas pa'i gzugs brnyan min / /
de yi ngo tsha'i rgod don dang / /
bdag nyid dga' ba'i don nyid du / /
bden min gyis kyang mi mo yi / /
rjes su 'jug pa rigs pa yin / /
yang dag 'dud dang rjes 'jug gi / /
bud med rnams kyis sems 'ching ste / /
brtse ba'i yon tan skye gnas phyir / /
yid la 'dod pa bud med yin / /
de phyir rnam par spangs pa'i spyan / /
snying la gzhan du phyir bltas kyang / /
'di yi yul dang rjes mthun par / /
mkhas pa rnam par dpyad par 'os / /
mkhas pa sman yin bud med la / /
mkhas pa rab mchog rgyan yin no / /
mkhas pa dang bral gzugs dag ni / /
me tog med pa'i nags dang 'dra / /
yang na mkhas pa'i rang bzhin gyi / /
bsam pa rang bzhin khas len mdzod / /
yul rnams nyes par dka' thob nas / /
phyi shol byed pa 'os ma yin / /

'dod pa mchog ces shes byas nas / /
gau tam thub pa'i dga' ldan ma / /
bshol med ma la 'dod pa byas / /
zla ba'i chung ma snar ma ni / /
drang srong ri byis don du gnyer / /
de nas de dang 'dra ba yi / /

u b+ha th+ya yi chung ma ni / /

ba ra dwa dza bskyed par gyur / /
drang srong phur bu'i chung ma ni / /
sbyin sreg ma la sbyin sreg mchog /
zla ba yis ni lag pa yi / /

sngon tshe bu mo nag mo ni / /

ya nu ni yi gling du phyin / /
gnod sbyin phreng ma rigs ngan ma / /
snod ma la ni dga' 'dod pas / /
gong ma sreg ni za ba'i bu / /
thub pa gnas mchog gis bskyed do / /
'gro mgyogs rgyal po drang srong nyid / /
na tshod rnam par song ba yi / /
lha mo sna tshogs mchod mar bcas / /
sna tshogs shing rta'i nags su dga' / /
bud med 'grogs min zhi ba ni / /
skya bseng gis ni shes nas kyang / /
dga' ma'i gzugs yon gyis bkug ste / /
'dod las skyes pa'i bde ba bsten / /
skyed mdzad rgyal po dmar ser yang / /

na babs thob pa nyid yin kyang / /

gal te 'di gsum ma yin na / /

rmongs las der ni dga' bar 'gyur / /

skyo ba med par rol pa ni / /
ri dgas dang ni bya dang mtshungs / /
bdag nyid chen po 'di rnams kyang / /

gang tshe de rnams kyi yang tshad / /
gang du phyi las zad pa ste / /
bdag nyid chen por mi sems te / /
yul rnams la ni chags pa 'am / /
sbyor min bdag nyid ldan nyid kyis / /
mkhas pa yis kyang dpe brjod cing / /

dngos po kun gyi tshogs ba de / /

mi brtan pa yi dad pa dang / /

chags pa skyes par gyur pa'i sems / /
slu bar bya ba ci zhig yin / /
bud med skyes pa'i chags skyes shing / /
bud med skyes pa phan tshun du / /
gal te de ltar slu na ni / /
lta bar nus pa nyid ma yin / /

nyam thag rga 'chi'i skal ba can / /

e ma shin tu brtan la stobs ldan khyod kyi sems / /
'dod pa g.yo ba rnams su snying po mthong gyur la / /
shin tu rno zhing 'jigs pa'i yul la zon mdzad cing / /
rga dang rgud pa nad kyi 'jigs pa rnam sems shing / /
'gro ba rnams ni me yis tshig pa bzhin thos na / /
zhi ba 'thob min brtan min dga' ba ga la zhig /
the tshom med par 'chi zhes rab tu shes pa yi / /
mi rnams gang gi snying la chags pa rab skyed pa / /
de yi sems ni lcags las gyur par shes pa ste / /
'jigs pa che la chags pa gang zhig du ba med / /
de nas gzhon nu yis ni 'dod pa rnams kyis bsten / /
'joms byed gtam ni rnam par nges pa'i bdag nyid mdzad / /
skye bo rnams kyi mig gi 'gro bya gsal byed kyi / /
dkyil 'khor sa 'dzin ri bo la ni nub par gyur / /
de nas rgyan dang me tog phreng ba 'bras med 'dzin / /
sgyu rtsal yon tan gyis dang rab dgas 'bras med rnams / /
rang gi sems la yid dkrugs 'dod pa rnams smad nas / /

de nas grong khyer skyed mos tshal song skye bo'i dpal / /
legs par brtags nas spyod la so sor brtul te yang / /

bud med kyis gegs byas pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o // //
de ltar yul rnams dam pa'i mchod pa rnams kyis ni / /
sred du bcug kyang shAkya'i rgyal po'i sras po de / /
dug bsgos mda' yis snying la phug pa'i seng ge bzhin / /
bde ba rnyed pa ma yin brtan par gshegs ma gyur / /
de nas res 'ga' zhig na blon po'i bu mkhas shing / /
grogs gyur sna tshogs gtam gyis rjes su 'brangs byas pa / /
nags kyi sa la 'gro 'dod lta bar 'dod pa yis / /
mi yi lha yis rjes gnang phyi rol rab tu gshegs / /
gsar ba'i gser gyi srab dang dril bu chung ngu dang / /
rab tu g.yo ba'i rnga yab mdzes pa'i gser sga dang / /
stan bcas dam pa'i rta la mngon par zhon nas ni / /
tog la ljon dang chu skyes tog can bzhin du gshegs / /
de ni mchog tu rnam par rgyang ring nags mtha'i sa / /
nags tshal 'dod dang sa yi yon tan las gshegs te / /
chu gnyer bzhin du rnam par bkram pa'i gshol lam can / /
nor 'dzin sa la zhing dag rmo ba gzigs par gyur / /

shi gyur 'bu srin srog chags phra mos khyab pa ste / /

rang gi skye bo bsad pa la bzhin mya ngan gyur / /

sa la rnam par rgyu zhing mya ngan dang ldan pa / /

rtog pa dpyod pa dang bcas zhi ba thob par gyur / /
rnam par dben pa las skyes thob nas de nas ni / /

nad pa dang ni shi dang rga bas nyam thag gam / /
gzhan la rgyags pas long zhing shes pa med pas smod / /

de ni yang dag mthong nas shAkya'i bu mo zhig /

bla ma spangs nas khyod kyi chos kyis chos ma yin / /

bud med kha cig grogs mo bzhin du gnyid log go / /
lang tsho ma gzhan lag pa'i dpung pa'i yul las ni / /
kun nas rnam 'phyang mdzes pa'i logs can pa Na wa / /
sgyeg bcas dga' ba'i mthar ni thang chad sdug pa bzhin / /
brla gnyis dag ni dbus su blangs nas nyal ba'o / /
rab tu yang dag 'khums gyur pad+ma dmar po'i mdzod / /
nyi ma nub par gyur tshe rdzing bu rnams ji ltar / /
rnam rgyas mig dang mdzes pa'i smin ma yod na yang / /
gzhan rnams mig rnams btsums shing mdzes par ma gyur to / /
de bzhin gzhan ni mgo skyes lhod pa las 'khrugs shing / /
rgyan dang dar rnams dpyi la rnam nyil de rnams ni / /
yan lag ma yi gzugs brnyan glang pos bcom pa bzhin / /

gzhan rnams kyang ni dbang med ngo tshas rnam spangs shing / /
rnam par 'gyur zhing bskyod pa'i yan lag gya gyu dang / /
dbugs ni rnam par rgyu zhing lus po gsal bar gnyid / /

mdud pa'i gos rnams rnam par nyil gyur 'du shes med / /
btsums pa ma yin dkar po g.yo ba dang bral mig /
srog song ro ltar nyal ba rnam par mdzes ma gyur / /
kha sbyar rnam par gdangs te lus po rab brkyang zhing / /

de ltar sems pa dang ni rigs kyi rjes 'gro'i gzugs / /

rdzing bu dang ni mtshungs pa'i gzugs ni mdzes par gyur / /
de ltar rnam par 'gyur la brtan min spyod pa can / /
de ltar nyal ba'i lang tsho ldan ma de mthong nas / /
lus kyi yon tan ldan zhing smra ba'i yid 'ong yang / /
mi skyong sras po des ni rnam par smad par gyur / /
mi gtsang rnam par 'gyur ba gson pa'i 'jig rten te / /
bud med rnams kyi rang gi ngo bo 'di 'dra ba / /
bgo ba rnams dang rgyan rnams kyis kyang slu ba ste / /
bud med rnams kyi yul la skyes pa chags par 'gro / /

rmi lam rnam par 'gyur ba bzhin du rnam dpyad na / /
nges par 'dir ni bag med 'phel ba ma yin la / /
'on kyang yon tan rtog pa bcom ste chags par 'gro / /
de ltar de yi go skabs rnam par rig nas ni / /
mtshan mor phyi ru 'gro 'dod yang dag skyes par gyur / /
'di yi sems ni kun nas rtog nas de nas ni / /

de nas lang tsho ldan ma nyal ba de rnams ni / /
smad cing de ni lding khang logs nas babs pa ste / /
mngon par babs nas de nas som nyi rnam bral bar / /

de ni mgyogs 'gro bsrungs la go bar byas nas ni / /
skyen par 'dun pa la ni 'di skad ces smras so / /
bsngags ldan rta ni khyer shog myur ba dang ldan pas / /

de bzhin 'khor los sgyur ba chung ma dang bcas pa / /
dbang po dang mtshungs de mthong song bar ma gyur to / /
sbyin sreg bud shing phyir ni bram ze rnams phyin nas / /
me tog lo 'dab rgyas pa'i lag pa gtsang ma rnams / /
dka' thub gtso bo rnams ni blo rnams byas na yang / /
gshegs pa mthong ste klog glar song bar ma gyur to / /
chu gter sngon po bzhin du mthong nas rma bya rnams / /
dga' zhing gyen du dud cing skad dag 'don gyur la / /
rgya skyegs ri dgas spyod ldan rnams dang ri dgas rnams / /
'bru rnams bor nas mngon par gdong phyogs gnas par gyur / /
'od zer ldan pa shar ba lta bur 'bar ba yis / /
bu ram shing pa'i rigs kyi sgron ma de mthong nas / /
sbyin sreg 'jo rnams bzhos pa yin na yang / /
rab tu dga' ba skyes te rab tu 'jo gyur to / /
'di ni nor sbyin rnams kyi brgyad pa yin nam ci / /
tha skar dag gi nang nas gcig ni 'phos sam zhes / /
de mthong ba la ya mtshan skyes par gyur pa yi / /
thub pa rnams kyi tshig der mthon por sgrogs bar gyur / /
lha yi khyu mchog gnyis pa'i lus po lta bu dang / /
'jig rten rgyu dang mi rgyu'i snying po lta bu dang / /
gang 'dod pa yis nyi ma mngon par babs 'dra ba / /
des ni nags tshal mtha' dag rab tu snang bar mdzod / /
de nas gdung gnas pa de rnams kyi ji lta bzhin / /
nye bar snyan gsan phab cing mngon par mchod gyur la / /
de ni chu bcas chu 'dzin lta bu'i dbyangs kyis ni / /
chos 'dzin rnams la slar yang rab tu mchod par gyur / /
de nas rnam par thar bzhed brtan pa de yis ni / /
dka' thub sna tshogs rnams la nges par rnam gzigs shing / /
mtho ris mngon 'dod bsod nams byas pa'i skye bo yis / /
khyab pa'i dka' thub gnas der rjes su dpyad par gyur / /
dka' thub nor can rnams kyi dka' thub nags tshal der / /
dka' thub rnam par 'gyur ba rnams ni nges gnas nas / /
rjes su gshegs pa'i dka' thub ldan pa kha cig la / /
zhi bas de nyid rnam par shes bzhed 'di gsungs so / /
gang phyir chos kyi cho ga 'di ni mi shes pa / /
bdag gis dka' thub gnas mthong de ring snga ma'o / /
de phyir khyod kyis bdag la smra bar 'os min te / /
nges pa gang zhig gang la rab tu 'jug pa'o / /
de nas dka' thub rnam par rgyu ba'i gnyis skyes des / /
shAkya'i khyu mchog khyu mchog rnam par gnon pa po / /
de la rim gyis dka' thub khyad par rnams dang ni / /
dka' thub 'bras bu dang bcas gtam ngag byas pa'o / /
grong byung bza' ba ma yin chu la rab skyes pa'i / /
'dab ma rnams dang chu dang 'bras bu rtsa ba nyid / /
thub pa rnams kyi spyod pa 'di ni lung ji ltar / /
dka' thub rnams kyi rnam rtog tha dad de de'o / /
kha cig ri dgas bzhin du rtswa rnams la spyod la / /
gzhan rnams bor ba yis ni mkha' la rgyu ba'i bya ltar 'tsho / /
kha cig lag 'gro rnams dang lhan cig 'tsho ba ste / /
grog mkhar gyur pa rnams ni nags na rlung gis so / /
rdo yis rab 'bad bsgrub pa'i spyod pa gzhan rnams te / /
kha cig rang gi so yis nye bar blangs shing za / /
de bzhin gzhan ni gzhan gyi don du bcos byas nas / /
gal te lhag ma yod na bya ba byed pa'o / /
chu yis gsher ba'i ral pa'i tshogs can kha cig ni / /
gsang sngags sngon 'gro lan gnyis me la sbyin sreg cing / /
kha cig nya dang mnyam par chu la rnams zhugs nas / /
rus sbal bzhin du lus rnams rab tu bskum pa'o / /
de ltar dus su bsags pa'i dka' thub nags tshogs kyi / /
mchog gis lhar 'gro gzhan gyis mi yi 'jig rten te / /
sdug bsngal lam gyis bde ba nye bar thob phyir dang / /
chos kyi rtsa ba bde ba nyid du gsungs phyir ro / /
de skad ces sogs rkang gnyis dbang po'i sras po yis / /
dka' thub nor dang ldan pa de yi tshig gsan nas / /
de nyid gzigs pa min yang ngoms par ma gyur la / /
bdag tu song ba 'di ni dal bus gsungs par gyur / /
sdug bsngal bdag nyid dka' thub rnam pa du ma ste / /
dka' thub bdag gi 'bras bu mtho ris gtso bo'o / /
'jig rten thams cad yongs su 'gyur ba dang ldan la / /
nyung ngu la ngal 'di ni gdung gnas rnams kyi'o / /
phangs pa rnams dang gnyen dang yul rnams bor nas ni / /
gang zhig mtho ris phyir ni rnam par spyod byed la / /
de rnams rnam par bral te nges par 'gro 'dod la / /
slar yang shin tu 'ching ba chen po nyid yin no / /
lus kyi ngal dub gdung ba'i bya ba rnams kyis ni / /
'dod pa'i rgyu las rab tu 'jug par 'dod pa'o / /
'khor ba'i rgya mtsho'i skyon rnams yongs su mi rtog par / /
sdug bsngal gyis de sdug bsngal kho na rjes su tshol / /
'chi bas skye dgu rnams kyis rtag par 'jigs pa ste / /
'bad pa yis ni slar yang rab tu 'jug par 'dod / /
rab tu zhugs par gyur na nges par 'chi ba ste / /
'di nyid du ni gang las 'jigs pa rnams lhung ngo / /
'di yi don du gcig rnams ngal bar rab 'jug cing / /
gzhan rnams mtho ris don du ngal ba 'thob pa ste / /
bde ba'i don du sred pa'i bkren pa don ma byas / /
gson pa'i 'jig rten nges par don med nyid du lhung / /
gang zhig dman pa dor nas khyad 'phags 'gro ba can / /
'bad pa 'di ni nges par smad pa ma yin la / /
shes ldan rnams dang mnyam pa'i yongs su gdung ba yis / /
bya ba ma yin de 'dir slar yang byed pa'o / /
lus kyi gtser bas gal te 'dir ni chos yin na / /
lus kyi bde ba chos ma yin par 'gyur ba ste / /
pha rol du ni bde ba chos kyis kyang 'thob la / /
de phyir 'di yis chos kyi chos min 'bras bu'o / /
gang gi phyir na bsams pa'i dbang gis lus yin la / /
rab tu 'jug pa dang ni zlog pa dag kyang ngo / /
de phyir sems kyi dul ba nyid ni rig pa ste / /
sems las gzhan pa'i lus ni shing dang mnyas ba'o / /
bza' ba gtsang bas gal te bsod nams 'dod na ni / /
de phyir ri dgas rnams kyang bsod nams yod pa ste / /
phyi rol skyes bu gang dag rnams kyang 'bras bu las / /
bskal pa'i nyes pas don rnams gzhan du kha bltas so / /
bsod nams phyir ni sdug bsngal mngon par mtshams sbyor na / /
'o na sdug bsngal mngon par mtshams sbyor tshad ma min / /
de ltar gang dag las ni rnam par dag pa'i phyir / /
stegs zhes rab tu zhugs te chu la reg par byed / /
de yang de yi snying la tshim pa tsam yin te / /
chu yis sdig pa dag par byed pa ma yin phyir / /
yon tan ldan bas rig pa'i chu ni gang dang gang / /
de dang de ni sa la gal te stegs 'dod na / /
chu yang the tshom med par chu nyid kho na ste / /
de phyir yon tan ldan rnams kho na stegs su go / /
de ltar rigs pa mang po ldan pa de dang de / /
smras te rnam par mdzes pa'i nyi ma nub bar gyur / /
de nas sbyin sreg du bas kha dog 'gyur ba'i shing / /
dka' thub rab tu zhi ba'i khrus sar rnam par zhugs / /
mngon par bton pa'i rab tu 'bar ba'i me yis thal ba ni / /
dbang bskur byas pa'i drang srong skye bos khyab pa ste / /
bzlas bya'i dbyangs kyis kun nas skad sgrogs lha yi tshogs / /
chos kyi lam gyi las kyi mtha' bzhin rab tu zhugs pa'o / /
de ni mtshan mo thang 'ga' mtshan mor byed 'od kyis / /
dka' thub rnams la yongs su rtog cing zhugs gyur la / /
dka' thub thams cad yongs su brtags shing mkhyen gyur na / /
dka' thub zhing gi thang de las ni gshegs par gyur / /
de'i gzugs bdag nyid chen por sod ba'i yid rnams kyis / /
dka' thub gnas ldan rnams ni de nas de rjes gshegs / /
'phags min sdig pa rnams kyis zil non yul las ni / /
drang srong chen po rnams ni chos bzhin pha rol gshegs / /
de nas ral pa shing shun zur phud kyis rol ba'i / /
dka' thub nor dang ldan ba de rnams des gzigs shing / /
de dag rnams kyis dka' thub rnams la rjes brten te / /
dpal dang ldan la dge ba'i shing gi rtsa bar gnas / /
de nas dka' thub gnas ldan rnams ni nyer 'ongs nas / /
mi mchog de la yongs su bskor nas gnas gyur la / /
de dag rnams kyi rgyan pos mchod ma sngon btang ste / /
dus kyi zhi bas tshig 'di rab tu 'di smras so / /
khyod kyis byon tshe gdung gnas gang ba bzhin gyur la / /
rab tu gshegs tshe stong pa bzhin du rab tu thob / /
de phyir brtse ba 'di ni 'bor bar 'os min te / /
'tsho bar 'dod pa'i phangs pa'i tshe yis lus bzhin no / /
lha yi drang srong tshangs pa'i drang srong rgyal po yis / /
drang srong gis bsnyen bsod nams nye bar gang ldan ri / /
dka' thub nor ldan rnams kyi dka' thub de rnams ni / /
gang gi nye logs dag nas mang por 'gyur ba'o / /
de bzhin kun nas bsod nams dag gi stegs gyur la / /
nam mkha'i 'og gi them skas dag tu gyur pa ste / /
lha yi drang srong rnams dang drang srong chen po ni / /
chos kyi bdag nyid bdag nyid chen po rnams kyis bsnyen / /
'di nas slar yang khyad 'phags chos kyi ched las ni / /
byang gi phyogs nyid kho nar bsnyen par nus pa ste / /
blo dang ldan pas gom pa gcig tu gyur pa yang / /
lho yi phyogs su 'gro bar nus pa ma yin no / /
dka' thub nags 'dir ji ste bya ba ngan pa 'am / /
bsre ma'i chos sam ltung ba min nam mi gtsang bar / /
khyed kyis mthong ste gang gis khyed 'di bzhugs 'dod min / /
de ni gsung la re zhig sred par bzhugs mdzod cig /
dka' thub gter dang rab tu mtshungs par gyur pa la / /
'di rnams kyis ni dka' thub grogs su 'dod pa ste / /
dbang po dang mnyam khyed dang lhan cig gnas pa ni / /
phur bu yi yang mngon par mtho ba 'dren pa yin / /
dka' thub ldan pa'i gtso bos de skad ces smras te / /
srid pa rab tu nyams phyir dam bca' byas pa yis / /
mkhas pa'i gtso bo des ni dka' thub ldan dbus su / /
nang du song ba'i rang bzhin smras par gyur pa'o / /
'gron la sdug cing rang gi skye bo dang mtshungs pa'i / /
drang po'i bdag nyid chos 'dzin thub pa rnams kyis ni / /
bdag la rnam pa de ltar bsam pa skyes pa yis / /
bdag gi dga' ba mchog dang bkur sti skyes par gyur / /
mdor bsdus gyur na brtse zhing bsnyen pa 'di rnams dag /
snying la song ba'i ngag rnams ngag gis khrus byas bzhin / /
kun nas 'dzin med chos can bdag gi dga' ba ni / /
de ring slar yang cung zhig g.yos par gyur pa nyid / /
de ltar rab tu zhugs pa'i khyed cag skyabs 'os rnams / /
shin tu phyogs su lhung ba yang dag bstan pa rnams / /
bor nas 'gro zhes kho bo yi yang sdug bsngal te / /
ji ltar gnyen 'dun rnams ni spangs pa de ltar ro / /
khyed cag rnams kyi chos 'di mtho ris ched du ste / /
bdag gi mngon par mtho bar yang srid ma yin phyir / /
nags der gang gi bdag ni sdod 'dod ma yin te / /
chos las ldog pa rab tu 'jug pa tha dad phyir / /
de phyir nags 'di dag na gang gis yongs 'gro ba / /
bdag gi ma dga' ma yin pha rol spyod log min / /
sngon gyi dus na rjes mthun chos la gnas pa yi / /
drang srong chen po thams cad rnams dang mtshungs par gyur / /
de nas don dang ldan la bde zhing yid du 'ong / /
legs mthun mdangs dang ldan la snying po dang ldan pa / /
gzhon nu'i tshig ni dka' thub ldan pa de rnams kyis / /
thos nas khyad 'phags dang ldan bkur sti mang pos gshegs / /
de nas gnyis skyes thal ba la nyal kha cig ni / /
lus ring gtsug tor dang ldan shing shun gos gyon zhing / /
mig ni cung zad dmar ser sna ni phra la rings / /
lag gcig spyi blugs ldan pas tshig 'di smras pa'o / /
khyod kyis nges pa nyid du rgya chen blo ldan zhing / /
gzhon nu khyed kyi skye ba la ni nyes pa gzigs / /
mtho ris dang ni nyes pa yang dag rnam spyod phyir / /
thar pa gang gi blo gros yod pa de yin no / /
mchod sbyin dka' thub nges ba de dang de rnams kyis / /
chags pa dang ldan mtho ris la ni 'gro bar 'dod / /
dgra bo bzhin du chags dang lhan cig g.yul sprad nas / /
sems pa rang ldan thar pa ru ni 'gro bar 'dod / /
de phyir gal te khyod kyi blo gros 'di nges na / /
skyen par khyed nyid 'bigs byed phug par gshegs mdzod cig / /
gang zhig mthar thug nges par legs pa thob ba'i mig / /
thub pa 'di ni de ru mtshan mo min par gnas / /
de phyir khyod kyis de nyid lam ni thob 'gyur la / /
sred par gyur na yang dag rab tu thob par 'gyur / /
bdag gi mthong ba ji ltar blo gros de de ltar / /
de nyid kyi yang blo gros bor nas 'gro bar 'gyur / /
gsal zhing mtho ba'i shangs dang rnam rgyas yangs pa'i spyan / /
zangs mdog ya mchu ma mchu rno dkar mche ba can / /
ljags ni dmar zhing phra ba'i zhal dang ldan pa 'di / /
shes bya'i rgya mtsho mtha' dag la ni 'gro ba nyid / /
khyod kyi zab pa dang ni gting dpag dka' gang dang / /
gang zhig sgron ma nyid dang mtshan rnams gang yin pas / /
sngon gyi bskal par drang srong gis kyang ma mthong ba'i / /
slob dpon nyid de sa la mngon par dga' nas gshegs / /
dka' thub ldan pa de rnams kyis kyang de la yang / /
cho ga bzhin rjes byas nas dka' thub nags der gshegs / /
sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las / /
dka' thub kyi nags su zhugs pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o // //
de nas mgyogs 'gro spyod de yid mi bde gyur te / /
de ltar jo bo nags su nga med par gshegs la / /
lam du mya ngan med pa 'bad pa byas gyur te / /
de lta na yang de yi mchi ma khogs ma gyur / /
gang la jo bo'i bka' la mtshan mo gcig gis ni / /
mgyogs 'gro de dang gshegs par gyur pa'i lam / /
lam de nyid la 'gro zhag dag ni brgyad rnams kyis / /
jo bo nyid dang bral ba de yis sems shing 'ongs / /
'thon ba med pas rgyags pa med par gyur pa yis / /
bsngags ldan mgyogs 'gro nyid kyang mdangs med rgyu ba ste / /
de ltar rgyan de rnams kyis brgyan par byas na yang / /
de yis dor bas dpal ni song ba bzhin du gyur / /
phyir log nas kyang dka' thub nags su mngon phyogs te / /
snying rje bar ni yang dang yang du drag tu 'tsher / /
lam na ltogs pa ldan pa yin yang 'bru dang chu / /
ji ltar sngon bzhin mngon par ma dga' ma bslangs so / /
de nas 'gro la phan pa'i bdag nyid bdag nyid chen po des / /
ser skya zhes bya'i grong khyer rnam par dman pa la / /
nyin mor byed pas bor ba'i nam mkha' 'bras med bzhin / /

pad+ma dkar po dang bcas chu yis mdzes gyur zhing / /
me tog 'dzin pa'i shing rnams kyis ni brgyan pa yang / /
grong khyer pa rnams rab tu dga' ba song gyur te / /
de yi nye ba'i nags de nags ltar mdzes ma gyur / /
de ltar lta byed mchi mas bcom pa'i mi rnams ni / /
rab tu 'bar min zhan pa'i yid kyis phyogs su skor / /
'ong du mi ster ba bzhin gnyis po de grong du / /
dal bus log pa'i khrus bzhin mngon par song bar gyur / /

lus zags 'gros dang ldan pa de gnyis mthong nas kyang / /
sngon tshe shing rta bcu pa'i shing rta 'ongs pa bzhin / /
grong khyer skye bo rnams ni lam du mchi ma phyung / /
de nas mya ngan nye bar ldan ba'i skye bo dag /
mchi ma byung ba rnams kyis 'dun pa la smras pa / /
grong khyer yul 'khor dga' mdzad rgyal bo'i sras po de / /
khyed kyis gang du bor zhes rgyab nas rjes su 'gro / /
de nas gus ldan skye bo de la des smras pa / /
mi dbang sras po bdag gis yongs su bor ba min / /
ngu bzhin skye bo med pa'i nags su kho bo dang / /
khyim bdag cha lugs dag kyang de yis rnam par spangs / /
de yi tshig ni skye bo de rnams kyis thos nas / /
nges par shin tu dka' ba nyid ces nges par song gyur la / /
'gyel zhing mig skyes chu ni rnam par 'thor ba ste / /
yid la smod cing bdag nyid kyis ni 'bras bu long / /
de nas smras pa gnyis skyes rgyal po'i shugs mnga' ste / /
gang du gshegs pa'i nags der di ring zhugs par bgyi / /
lus can dbang po ma tshang rnams kyi ji lta bar / /
de dag bral bas bdag cag 'tshe bar 'dod pa med / /
de dang bral ba'i grong khyer 'di ni nags yin la / /
de dang yang dag ldan pa'i nags de grong khyer yin / /
lha ni lha min gsod tshe brgya byin gyis ji ltar / /
de dag bral bas bdag gi grong khyer mdzes ma gyur / /
de nas slar yang gzhon nu phyir la log ces te / /
yan lag ma rnams skar khung phreng rnams rab thob ste / /
mgyogs 'gro'i rgyab ni rnam par dben ba mthong gyur nas / /
slar yang skar khung rnams ni rnam par bkag nas ngu / /
brtul zhugs dang ni mya ngan dag gis yid dub cing / /
brtul zhugs la rab zhugs pas sras po nyer thob phyir / /
bzlas byas shing gi lha yi khang par mi bdag gis / /
bsam pa ji ltar bya ba de dang de rnams byas / /
de nas mig dag mchi mas rab tu gang ba des / /
mgyogs 'gro blangs nas mgyogs 'gro rjes su 'gro ba ste / /
g.yul 'gyed pa na dgra bos jo bo khyer ba ltar / /
mya ngan dag gis mngon bcom mi skyong khang par zhugs / /
mi dbang rgyal po'i khab tu rnam par zhugs pa na / /
rnam par blta zhing mig dag mchi ma 'bab pa yis / /

bsngags ldan mgyogs 'gro gsal ba'i dbyangs kyis ngus par gyur / /

ji ltar bsngags ldan mgyogs 'gro 'tsher bar byed pa ste / /

dga' ba phul du byung bas bslus pa'i skye bo rnams / /
skye bo'i bdag po'i btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nye logs song / /

bud med rnams ni sred pas khyim nas phyir la 'thon / /
lan bu rnam par 'phyang zhing dar gos dri ma can / /
mig rtsi dang bral mchi mas mig bcom gdong rnams kyis / /

byi dor dang bral bud med rid rnams mdzes ma gyur / /

nu ma do shal dang bral stod g.yogs tshad rnams so / /

nags mthar khyu mchog dang bral ba glang rnams bzhin du / /
sems khral gdong ldan yan lag mchog ma rnams ni ngus / /
de nas rgyal po'i btsun mo mchi ma dang bcas par / /
be'u nyams pa'i ma he mo ltar mnyes gshin ma / /
gser gyi chu shing lo 'dab rnam par g.yo ba bzhin / /

bud med gzhan rnams yid mi bde bas sems med bzhin / /

sa 'dzin ri bo nas 'bab rgyun gyi rdo ba ltar / /

de rnams kyis ni mig chus btab pa'i gdon rnams kyis / /

rlung gis g.yos pa'i ljon shing rang gi 'dab mas ltar / /
